 I believe the meaning of life is to do with helping other people. In my opinion, we are put on this earth for a reason and our own personal reasons can be fulfilled by giving back too others who need help or have fallen upon tough times. Helping your neighbours when they’re struggling through hardships such as illness/financial problems etc brings about the feeling of helping them to get over those obstacles in their life, thus freeing ourselves from unnecessary worries and stresses!
The word ‘meaningful’ is often associated with something that has a specific purpose. For instance we may say; “I went on a meaningless holiday”. This statement suggests there was no aim or goal behind the trip so it could be labelled as unimportant, pointless etc.. I think meaningful things are like this in comparison to everyday life – they have an end result and/or significance which makes them worthwhile.
A person’s sense of purpose is often linked with their job; for example if someone was unhappy at work because everything felt like it was meaningless then perhaps there would be no point spending time doing things that wouldn’t make any difference in terms of what they wanted from life? This isn’t always possible though as sometimes you need money even if your job may not provide enough ful

 I believe the meaning of life is to make other people smile.
We all have our own struggles, but we are not alone in this struggle through it all; you always find someone who shares your feelings and understands what's going on inside for us (maybe ourselves). It can be hard at times when things get rough or just plain terrible around the world where violence is a common occurrence. We should never give up hope because God will shine his light down upon our lives like stars in night sky, guiding you to find your way back home again once more - and forever after that too..
I am an African American male who grew up poor on Chicago's South side of the city; I know what it means. There are many people out there with no one they can count for or anyone taking care about them because their family members don't give a flying fuck either way - and if that happens then you just might as well be dead already in my opinion too..
But even though this kind of thinking has become so commonplace among those who live here still today; we have people like myself from all races/ethnicities coming together to change the mindsets about what's really going on behind closed doors where nobody gives two shits either way - but if you try hard enough maybe

You can do anything you want as long as it's legal and safe, but if you choose doing something that makes people uncomfortable or unsafe then obviously your not having any fun. If someone goes through school hating it because they think their supposed to learn things for a test instead of learning new skills so when life hits them in the face later on down the road its easier for success is I'd say no one has fun there and even if you do get good grades at least your not having much fun while doing homework or studying. As far as my parents go, they never forced me to do anything that made school harder than it had to be so therefore i did what wanted instead of just going through the motions for them like some people choose too . There's no reason why you can't have both and still pass all your classes with good grades.
I think we are here on earth because our soul needs experience, that is fun! We learn in school or college so it makes us more educated about life but its not the real world as some people believe to be; therefore if they want a job thats where this education comes into play and also I guess you can enjoy being at work too.

 I believe the meaning of life is to give, serve and love. My mission in this world is two-fold: 1) To help as many people make a difference through service & giving;and most importantly2)To be my own best human being...not always easy but well worth it!
Inspired by The Dalai Lama's quote on life, I live every day with the goal to inspire others and myself. If your not at least smiling you have no reason too:) This philosophy has helped me in all areas of personal growth & development as both a child and an adult-I am most happy when making someone smile!
"Everyone needs to serve something or else they will be miserable." ~The Dalai Lama~ Inspirational Quote on Life. (Photo by) I want my children not only to have fun but also learn the value of giving, respecting others and being grateful for what we do have-I believe that is a huge part in living your best life...and having an "attitude" of gratitude will change how you feel about yourself!

 I believe the meaning of life is to find out who we are and why we’re here.
Therefore, in my opinion: what people fear most isn’t death or anything like that but loss of self-identity (aka losing our inner being), something with which many philosophers agree as well! It seems there may be a connection between religion & philosophy…in some way they are similar ideas; however I don’t believe them to work together and neither do most people in my country, Japan.
I have been told by others that the meaning of life has nothing but happiness —but this is untrue because even if someone achieves complete bliss he/she can never be happy unless something bad happens…then it becomes a cycle; good times & then sadness (and vice versa). But I suppose there must come some point where people just give up trying to find meaning or live happily ever after.
I think the best way is not knowing what’s next for you, but rather taking your time figuring out which path/life journey suits one well enough! You can never plan too far ahead; this means being content with all aspects of life at any given moment: past & future alike (although it might sound easy).
Now we have a choice to make. Do what

 I believe the meaning of life is to discover your gift. The purpose of life is to give it away, said Pablo Picasso and he was right because after all giving comes before getting in God’s scheme for humanity as we see revealed through Jesus (Hebrew 13:20).
This means that you must first be willingly submitted to the gift within yourself. This does not come easily but it is a decision or choice between life and death…life with Christ, our Father; death without Him in which case all hell breaks loose on this Earth (Isaiah 57:18). The latter will have you at odds of being judged by God Almighty for your sin(s) because there are no exceptions.
Life is a gift from the Lord that comes with its own expectations and conditions like marriage, children, etc…but it’s all good because life in Christ Jesus gives us an opportunity to live again as we were created (John 3:16). This means accepting your God given nature of becoming who He wants you to be.
As a child there are certain gifts that may not have been discovered until much later, but the Lord knows what he is doing and will give them back in time according to His infinite wisdom…this

 I believe the meaning of life is to make someone happy and if you are not making anyone, then why do it?
I am an old 21 year-old man. It's pretty hard for me because people see a young soul inside with energy coming out from my ears like electricity when they meet me but I know that time goes by so quickly since the day of birth until now and in this short life journey, sometimes you wonder if it was worth?
I used to think about what is happiness. If there's one thing worse than being bored or tired (which are feelings every human experiences), feeling like your heart will explode out of excitement would be perfect for me because I can always find a reason on why that happened and how did they make my life better today?
That was the first time when happiness came to this world. No one knew what it meant, but we all know its existence now as an important feeling in our lives. When something makes you feel alive or complete is probably your happy moment because everything around us has no meaning if not for having a reason on why should be here and how did they make their presence valuable?
I think that happiness will only come to humans who are able of understanding what it means without knowing anything about emotions, feelings when we

 I believe the meaning of life is to give yourself in all you do, and that’s what we strive for at L.A. POWERLIFTING
I think this was one day when our coach got a bit carried away with telling us his theory about how he thought every man should look like Arnold Schwarzenegger if they wanted to get stronger or bigger because there are no shortcuts and it’s all hard work! “We never say 5 sets of 3, we only do 1 set of 10!”
The boys were still in school but I was the older one so had taken on more responsibility than them. One day my brother dropped out to join a band because he couldn’t live with his parents anymore and they moved back home while dad was away for business, leaving me alone at night when mum went to bed .
I remember being about 14 years old or something like that I had just got some new shoes from the shops after saving up all year. There were only two other guys in our class who lifted but we always wanted more than them so tried and tried every day for hours on end, even through lunch sometimes! We would also do a lot of walking around school together at break time or during lessons if there was nothing else

 I believe the meaning of life is to have a sense and purpose for one’s existence. The way that we can do this, in my mind anyways, is by using our time on Earth wisely – being kind to ourselves (and other people), focusing efforts where they will make us happy instead of just making money or doing things that feel good at the moment but not really fulfilling and helping others who are less fortunate than you.
But it also seems like there’s another part: when we die, what happens? Where do our souls go after they leave their bodies (which is a little terrifying to think about)? We know for sure because of one particular person that has shown us the way… and this story was told to me by my friend who goes on long walks every day without fail at some point in his journey.
He said, “There used to be two brothers living together as roommates when they were younger. One night while walking through their neighborhood late at night (not that it matters if you do), the older brother sees something moving near a tree ahead of him… he decides not to stop and turns back home but then realizes what happened and starts running towards where his brother was just standing by himself in such darkness.”
The younger brother had been playing with his
